abanticus, Salmo trutta Tortonese [E.] 1954:19, Pl. 1 (fig. 3); Figs. 2, 3a-b [Publications Institute Hydrobiology University of Istanbul (Sér. B) v. 2 (no. 1); ref. 12668] Lake Abant, northern Anatolia, Asiatic Turkey. Holotype (unique): MSNM 1 [ex MSNM 5031]. •Listed -- (Kottelat 1997:144 [ref. 22952]). •Synonym of Salmo labrax Pallas 1814 -- (Fricke et al. 2007:55 [ref. 29533]). •Synonym of Salmo trutta Linnaeus 1758 -- (Kalayci et al. 2018:803 [ref. 36785]). •Valid as Salmo abanticus Tortonese 1954 -- (Turan et al. 2010:362 [ref. 30689], Turan et al. 2011:32 [ref. 31466], Turan et al. 2012:234 [ref. 32276], Turan et al. 2014:285 [ref. 33242], Turan et al. 2014:149 [ref. 33615], Çiçek et al. 2015:150 [ref. 35151], Turan et al. 2017:62 [ref. 35485], Çiçek et al. 2018:21 [ref. 36267], Çiçek et al. 2020:255 [ref. 37644]). Current status: Valid as Salmo abanticus Tortonese 1954. Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Distribution: Asia Minor: Abant Gölü, Bolu Province, northwestern Anatolia (Turkey); introduced in Black Sea watersheds. Habitat: freshwater, brackish, marine.

adirondakus, Salmo Norris [T.] 1864:255, Fig. [The American angler's book, 1st edition; ref. 18479] Adirondack Lakes, New York, U.S.A. No types known. Also appeared as new in Norris 1865, 2nd edition, p. 255, fig. [ref. 31824] but spelled adirondacus. •Synonym of Salvelinus namaycush (Walbaum 1792) -- (Smith 1986:238 [ref. 22186], La Rivers 1994:257 [ref. 23389]). Current status: Synonym of Salvelinus namaycush (Walbaum 1792). Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Habitat: freshwater.

adriatica, Trutta Kolombatović [G.] 1890:166 [4] [Glasnik Hrvatskoga Naravoslovnoga Društva v. 5; ref. 20232] Vranjic, Croatia, Adriatic Sea, Mediterranean Sea. Holotype (unique): whereabouts unknown. On p. 4 of separate. •Questionably a synonym of Salmo marmoratus Cuvier 1829 -- (Kottelat 1997:138 [ref. 22952], Bianco 2013:3 [ref. 32897]). Current status: Uncertain as Salmo marmoratus Cuvier 1829. Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Habitat: freshwater, brackish, marine.

aegyptius, Salmo Gmelin [J. F.] (ex Forsskål) 1789:1386 [Caroli a Linné ... Systema Naturae per regna tria naturae v. 1 (pt 3); ref. 18139] Nile River, Egypt. No types known. Based on misidentification of Salmo niloticus (non Linnaeus 1758) in Forsskål 1775:xiii, 66 [ref. 1351] (see Fricke 2008: 17[ref. 30182]). Spelled Salmo aegyptiacus by Walbaum 1792:83 [ref. 4572], in synonymy of Salmo niloticus. •Synonym of Distichodus nefasch (Bonnaterre 1788) -- (Fricke 2008:18 [ref. 30182]). Current status: Synonym of Distichodus nefasch (Bonnaterre 1788). Distichodontidae. Habitat: freshwater.

aestivalis, Salmo ischchan var. Fortunatov [D.] 1926:243 [Izvestiya Otdela prikladnoi ikhtiologii v. 4 (no. 2); ref. 19992] Lake Sevan, Armenia. Syntypes: whereabouts unknown. •Synonym of Salmo ischchan Kessler 1877 -- (Berg 1948:261 [ref. 12882], Dorofeeva 1998:442 [ref. 24680] as infrasp. aestivalis). •Synonym of Salmo ischchan Kessler 1877, but a valid subspecies as described -- (Gabrielyan 2001:25 [ref. 25867]). Current status: Synonym of Salmo ischchan Kessler 1877. Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Habitat: freshwater.

aestivalis, Salmo letnica Stefanovic [D.] 1948:190, 2 figs. [Posebna izdanja / Srpska akademija nauka i umetnosti. Beograd 139; ref. 23038] Lake Ohrid, Republic of Macedonia. No types known. Objectively invalid; preoccupied by Salmo ischchan aestivalis Fortunatov 1927; replaced by Salmo aphelios Kottelat 1997. •Synonym of Salmo aphelios Kottelat 1997 -- (Kottelat & Freyhof 2007:420 [ref. 29996]). 1°Homonym. Current status: Synonym of Salmo aphelios Kottelat 1997. Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Habitat: freshwater.

agassizii, Salmo Garman [S.] 1885:20, Figs. 17-18 [Annual Report of the Commissoners of Inland Fisheries, Massachusetts v. 19 (no. 25) (for 1884); ref. 17931] Dublin Pond; Lake Monadnock, Keene; and Center Pond, New Hampshire, U.S.A. Syntypes: MCZ 7142 (1), 7147 (4), 25711 (5, now 4); NRM 25064 [ex MCZ 25771] (1). •Valid as Salvelinus agassizii (Garman 1885) -- (Lee et al. 1980:110 [ref. 22416] as agassizi). •Synonym of Salmo fontinalis (Mitchill 1814), but a valid subspecies agassizii Garman 1885 -- (Scharpf 2006:34 [ref. 30386], Page & Burr 2011:396 [ref. 31215]). Current status: Valid as Salvelinus agassizii (Garman 1885). Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Distribution: New Hampshire, U.S.A. [now extinct]. Habitat: freshwater.

aguabonita, Salmo mykiss Jordan [D. S.] 1892:62, Pl. [Biennial Report of the State Board of Fish Commissioners of the State of California (1891-1892); ref. 12346] "Volcano or Whitney Creek", Cottonwood lakes eastern side of Mt. Whitney, California, U.S.A. Syntypes: CAS-SU 514 (1), USNM 44237 (2). Type catalog: Böhlke 1953:15 [ref. 12291]. Originally as agua bonita. Also appeared in Jordan 1893:481 [ref. 10490]. •Synonym of Oncorhynchus mykiss (Walbaum 1792), but a valid subspecies -- (Behnke 1992:187 [ref. 23385], Stearley & Smith 1993:21 [ref. 26683], Moyle 2002:272 [ref. 26449], Scharpf 2006:30 [ref. 30386]). •Valid as Salmo aquabonita Jordan 1892 -- (Lee et al. 1980:103 [ref. 22416], La Rivers 1994:317 [ref. 23389]). •Valid as Oncorhynchus aguabonita (Jordan 1892) -- (McAllister 1990:83 [ref. 14674], Page & Burr 1991:55 [ref. 18983], Baxter & Stone 1995:160 [ref. 23374], Sigler & Sigler 1996:166 [ref. 25943], Fuller et al. 1999:243 [ref. 25838], Wydoski & Whitney 2003:55 [ref. 27816], Minckley & Marsh 2009:92 [ref. 31114], Page & Burr 2011:414 [ref. 31215] with 2 subspecies, Page et al. 2013:86 [ref. 32708], Penaluna et al. 2016:291 [ref. 34726]). Current status: Valid as Oncorhynchus aguabonita (Jordan 1892). Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Distribution: Western U.S.A. (originally California only). Habitat: freshwater, brackish, marine.

akairos, Salmo Delling [B.] & Doadrio [I.] 2005:58, Figs. 7-8 [Ichthyological Exploration of Freshwaters v. 16 (no. 1); ref. 28211] Lake Ifni, 31°01'59"N, 7°52'59"W, Morocco. Holotype: MNCN 115022. Paratypes: MNCN 115018-21, 115023-44 (?26, not 27), MNCN 115020 (head, c&s, as NRM 51752). •Valid as Salmo akairos Delling & Doadrio 2005 -- (Doadrio et al. 2015:9 [ref. 33950]). Current status: Valid as Salmo akairos Delling & Doadrio 2005. Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Distribution: Lake Ifni, Morocco. Habitat: freshwater.

alba, Salmo faria var. Meidinger [C. von] 1785-94:iv, Pl. 46 [Icones piscium Austriae indigenorum, quos collegit vivisque coloribus espresos edidit C. Baro de Meidinger.; ref. 17632] Austria. alpinostagnalis, Salmo Smitt [F. A.] 1886:111 et seq., 163, Pl. 3 (figs. 41-46) [Kongliga Vetenskaps-Academiens Handlingar, Stockholm v. 21 (no. 8); ref. 18730] Godthaab and Godhavn, Greenland. alpinus, Salmo Linnaeus [C.] 1758:309 [Systema Naturae, Ed. X v. 1; ref. 2787] "Lapponiae, Angliae alpibus, folus." No types known. See Kottelat & Freyhof 2009:82 [ref. 30320] for nomenclatural issues resulting in umbla Linnaeus taking precedence over alpinus Linnaeus for central and northern European charrs; alpinus is in prevailing usage and therefore retained. •Valid as Salvelinus alpinus (Linnaeus 1758) -- (Berg 1948:267 [ref. 12882], Svetovidov 1973:147 [ref. 7169], Lee et al. 1980:111 [ref. 22416], Svetovidov in Whitehead et al. 1984:383 [ref. 13675], Robins & Ray 1986:77 [ref. 23100], Lelek 1987:122 [ref. 22962], Scott & Scott 1988:137 [ref. 25518], McAllister 1990:85 [ref. 14674], Lloris & Rucabado 1991:53 [ref. 22530], Page & Burr 1991:49 [ref. 18983], Stearley & Smith 1993:21 [ref. 26683], López et al. 1996:16 [ref. 23681], Chereshnev 1996:604 [ref. 24659], Reshetnikov et al. 1997:729 [ref. 24702], Kottelat 1997:152 [ref. 22952], Dorofeeva & Savvaitova 1998:37 [ref. 23574], Scott & Crossman 1998:201 [ref. 24570], Alexeev & Pichugin 1998:328 [ref. 24677], Fuller et al. 1999:260 [ref. 25838], Bogutskaya et al. 2001:46 [ref. 26178], Chereshnev et al. 2001:94 [ref. 26736], Mecklenburg et al. 2002:199 [ref. 25968], Hanel 2003:58 [ref. 27894], Nelson et al. 2004:86 [ref. 27807], Bogutskaya & Naseka 2004:159 [ref. 28183], Duhamel et al. 2005:114 [ref. 32059], Scharpf 2006:33 [ref. 30386] with subspecies, Kottelat & Freyhof 2007:433 [ref. 29996], Oleinik & Skurichina 2007:911 [ref. 31791], Møller et al. 2010:27 [ref. 31169], Page & Burr 2011:396 [ref. 31215] with 3 subspecies, Page et al. 2013:87 [ref. 32708], Dolgov 2013:916 [ref. 33112], Parin et al. 2014:139 [ref. 33547], Oleinik et al. 2015:Eng. 62 [ref. 33831] as S. alpinus alpinus, Afonso et al. 2016:23, 270 [ref. 36199], Çiçek et al. 2015:150 [ref. 35151], Ćaleta et al. 2019:180 [ref. 37026], Dyldin et al. 2020:84, 103 [ref. 37569]). Current status: Valid as Salvelinus alpinus (Linnaeus 1758). Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Distribution: Arctic Ocean basin: circumpolar; North America and northern Europe; introduced elsewhere. Habitat: freshwater, brackish, marine.

altivelis, Salmo (Plecoglossus) Temminck [C. J.] & Schlegel [H.] 1846:229, Pl. 105 (figs. 1, 1a-c) [Fauna Japonica Parts 10-14; ref. 4374] Japan. Lectotype: RMNH 3179. Paralectotypes: RMNH D1971 (1, stuffed), D2414 (1, stuffed), 3179b-e (4, stuffed); ZMB 4114 [ex RMNH] (1). Type catalog: Paepke 2001:331 [ref. 25566]. Lectotype selected by Boeseman 1947:170 [ref. 12876]. •Valid as Plecoglossus altivelis, subspecies altivelis (Temminck & Schlegel 1846) -- (Zhang et al, 2016:187 [ref. 34477], Sonoyama et al. 2020:23 [ref. 37637]). •Valid as Plecoglossus altivelis (Temminck & Schlegel 1846) -- (Dyldin et al. 2020:99 [ref. 37569]). Current status: Valid as Plecoglossus altivelis (Temminck & Schlegel 1846). Plecoglossidae. Distribution: East Asia: mainland Japan, Peninsula of Korea, northern Vietnam. Habitat: freshwater, brackish, marine.

alvordensis, Salmo clarkii Sigler [W. F.] & Sigler [J. W.] 1987:357 [Fishes of the Great Basin: a natural history; ref. 23386] Appeared as "Alvord cutthroat trout S. c. alvordensis (undescribed)". The subspecies should date to Sigler & Sigler in our opinion. From Humboldt Co., Nevada, U.S.A. Behnke 1992:126 [ref. 23385] wrongly regarded it a nomen nudum, but states, "... and is an appropriatae name for this subspecies. Behnke 2002 gave himself credit for describing this subspecies, but we do not agree with this. •A valid, unnamed subspecies, but probably extinct as a pure form -- (Behnke 1992:126 [ref. 23385]). •Synonym of Oncorhynchus clarkii (Richardson 1836), but a valid subspecies alvordensis Sigler & Sigler 1987 -- (Scharpf 2006:26 [ref. 30386], Page & Burr 2011:409 [ref. 31215], Penaluna et al. 2016:291 [ref. 34726]). •Synonym of Oncorhynchus henshawi (Gill & Jordan 1878). Current status: Synonym of Oncorhynchus henshawi (Gill & Jordan 1878). Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Distribution: Southern Oregon and northern Nevada, U.S.A. [subspecies alvordensis, now extinct]. Habitat: freshwater.

americanus, Salmo Bloch [M. E.] & Schneider [J. G.] 1801:410 [M. E. Blochii, Systema Ichthyologiae; ref. 471] America. Family placement may be incorrect. Salmonidae: Salmoninae.

americanus, Salmo salar Payne [R. H.], Child [A. R.] & Forrest [A.] 1971:251 [Nature (London) v. 231 (no. 5300); ref. 863] North America. Unneeded new subspecific name for stocks of Atlantic salmon spawning in North American rivers; correct subspecific name should be the first species or subspecies of the Atlantic salmon based on a North American specimen. •Mention -- (Dorofeeva & Savvaitova 1998:35 [ref. 23574]). •Also preoccupied by Salmo americanus Bloch & Schneider 1801. 1°Homonym. Current status: Synonym of Salmo. Salmonidae: Salmoninae.

Type information: Wheeler 1989:212, Fig. 3A [ref. 21873]. •Valid as Anostomus anostomus (Linnaeus 1758) -- (Ortega & Vari 1986:12 [ref. 9708], Garavello & Britski in Reis et al. 2003:72 [ref. 27061], Garavello & Britski in Reis et al. 2003:72 [ref. 27061], Sidlauskas & Santos 2005:121 [ref. 28904], Sidlauskas & Vari 2008:74 [ref. 29786], Barriga Salazar 2014:105 [ref. 35745], DoNascimiento et al. 2017:39 [ref. 35633]). Current status: Valid as Anostomus anostomus (Linnaeus 1758). Anostomidae. Distribution: Amazon and Orinoco River basins: Brazil, Ecuador, Colombia, Guyana, Peru and Suriname. Habitat: freshwater.

apache, Salmo Miller [R. R.] 1972:403, Figs. 2-3 [Copeia 1972 (no. 3); ref. 7631] East fork of White River, Apache County, Arizona, U.S.A. Holotype: UMMZ 162769. Paratypes: ASU 5557 (35); CAS 27174 (13); UMMZ 121654 (3 or 4), 157653 (6), 162770 (32, 1 c&s), 189634 (23, 1 c&s), 189638 (20), 190814 (12); USNM 15999 (3). Other material: ASU (1 lot), CAS (6 lots), CAS-SU (1 lot), UMMZ (5 lots). •Valid as Salmo apache Miller 1972 -- (Lee et al. 1980:104 [ref. 22416], Rinne & Minckley 1985:285 [ref. 22488]). •Synonym of Oncorhynchus gilae (Miller 1950), but a valid subspecies -- (Behnke 1992:217 [ref. 23385], Stearley & Smith 1993:21 [ref. 26683], Scharpf 2006:27 [ref. 30386]). •Valid as Oncorhynchus apache (Miller 1972) -- (Rinne 1990:189 [ref. 36245], Page & Burr 1991:54 [ref. 18983], Minckley & Marsh 2009:83 [ref. 31114], Page & Burr 2011:415 [ref. 31215], Page et al. 2013:86 [ref. 32708], Penaluna et al. 2016:291 [ref. 34726]). Current status: Valid as Oncorhynchus apache (Miller 1972). Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Distribution: Arizona, U.S.A. Habitat: freshwater.

aphelios, Salmo Kottelat [M.] 1997:133 [Biologia (Bratislava) v. 52 (suppl. 5); ref. 22952] New name for Salmo letnica aestivalis Stefanovic 1948, preoccupied by Salmo ischchan aestivalis Fortunatov 1927. •Valid as Salmo aphelios Kottelat 1997 -- (Kottelat & Freyhof 2007:420 [ref. 29996]). The spelling ishikawae is acceptable; early workers almost certainly Latinized the name first, and then added an 'e' (Art. 31.1.1) [WNE, 12 Mar. 2012]. •Synonym of Oncorhynchus masou (Brevoort 1856) -- (Berg 1948:202 [ref. 12882] as masu, Okada 1961:317 [ref. 6363], see also Dorofeeva & Savvaitova 1998:33 [ref. 23574]). •Synonym of Salmo masou Brevoort 1856, but a valid subspecies -- (Kawanabe & Mizuno 1989:180 [ref. 25598]). •Synonym of Oncorhynchus masou (Brevoort 1856), but a valid subspecies ishikawae -- (Sato et al. 1998:38 [ref. 24972], Mizuno et al. 1999:7 [ref. 25311], Nakabo 2000:304 [ref. 25086], Matsuura et al. 2000:24 [ref. 26000], Shimizu 2001:21 [ref. 25799], Nakabo 2002:304 [ref. 26001], Gwo et al. 2008:778 [ref. 31607], Kano et al. 2010:78 [ref. 33818]). Current status: Synonym of Oncorhynchus masou (Brevoort 1856). Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Distribution: Southern areas of the Japanese Archipelago [this subspecies]. Habitat: freshwater, brackish, marine.

lavaretus, Coregonus Valenciennes [A.] (ex Cuvier) in Cuvier & Valenciennes 1848:466 [Histoire naturelle des poissons v. 21; ref. 1013] Perhaps only intended as a new combination, but Salmo lavaretus Linnaeus 1758 not mentioned by Valenciennes in description or in table of contents, so above description is regarded as subjectively invalid; unavailable, preoccupied in Coregonus by Salmo lavaretus Linnaeus 1758. Based on literature sources and one specimen from Geneva. 2°Homonym. Salmonidae: Coregoninae. Habitat: freshwater.

Syntypes: USNM 2070 (1), 2073 (1). •Synonym of Oncorhynchus nerka (Walbaum 1792) -- (Okada 1961:301 [ref. 6363]). •Synonym of Oncorhynchus tshawytscha (Walbaum 1792) -- (La Rivers 1994:247 [ref. 23389], Scott & Crossman 1998:177 [ref. 24570]). Current status: Synonym of Oncorhynchus tshawytscha (Walbaum 1792). Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Habitat: freshwater, brackish, marine.

wartmanni, Salmo Bloch [M. E.] 1784:161, Pl. 105 [M. Marcus Elieser Bloch's ..., ausübenden Arztes zu Berlin, Oeconomische Naturgeschichte der Fische Deutschlands v. 3; ref. 19645] Lake Constance, Europe. Holotype (unique): ZMB (lost). On p. 137 of Bloch's Ichthyologie, v. 3 [ref. 21381]. Spelled vartmanni by Bonnaterre 1788:166 [ref. 4940]. •Mention -- (Reshetnikov 1998:44 [ref. 23570]). •Valid as Coregonus wartmanni (Bloch 1784) -- (Kottelat 1997:113 [ref. 22952], Bianco & Ketmaier 2001:200 [ref. 26728], Kottelat & Freyhof 2007:364 [ref. 29996], Çiçek et al. 2015:150 [ref. 35151] as wartmani, Selz et al. 2020:151 [ref. 37901]). Current status: Valid as Coregonus wartmanni (Bloch 1784). Salmonidae: Coregoninae. Distribution: Upper basin of Lake Constance: Switzerland, Germany and Austria; introduced elsewhere. Habitat: freshwater.

whitehousei, Salmo kamloops Dymond [J. R.] 1931:393 [3] [Contributions to Canadian Biology and Fisheries (n. s.) v. 6 (no. 16); ref. 16269] Six-mile lake near Nelson, British Columbia, Canada. Holotype: ROM 6053. Paratypes: (19) UMMZ 9545 (1). On p. 3 of separate. •Synonym of Salmo gairdnerii Richardson 1836 -- (Scott & Crossman 1998:191 [ref. 24570] as gairdneri). •Now regarded as a synonym of Oncorhynchus mykiss (Walbaum 1792). Current status: Synonym of Oncorhynchus mykiss (Walbaum 1792). Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Habitat: freshwater, brackish, marine.

whitei, Salmo Evermann [B. W.] 1906:20, Pl. 16 [Bulletin of the Bureau of Fisheries v. 25 (for 1905); ref. 12306] South fork of Kaweah River in South Fork Meadows, Sierra, California, U.S.A. Holotype: USNM 53065. Paratypes: CAS-SU 9254 (1); USNM 53399 (2), 126744 [ex USBF 1252] (1). Additional material: ANSP 38037-39 (3); CAS 60533 [ex IU 11114] (1), 60534 [ex IU 11113] (1), 60535 [ex IU 11112] (4); CAS-SU 9831 (1); UMMZ 157677-79 (1, 1, 1); USNM 53458 (1). Type catalog: Böhlke 1953:15 [ref. 12291], Böhlke 1984:150 [ref. 13621]. •Synonym of Oncorhynchus mykiss (Walbaum 1792), subspecies gilberti (Jordan 1894) -- (Behnke 1992:191 [ref. 23385]). •Synonym of Oncorhynchus mykiss (Walbaum 1792), but a valid subspecies whitei (Evermann 1906) -- (Moyle 2002:272 [ref. 26449], Scharpf 2006:31 [ref. 30386]). •Synonym of Oncorhynchus aguabonita (Jordan 1892), but a valid subspecies whitei -- (Page & Burr 2011:414 [ref. 31215]). Current status: Synonym of Oncorhynchus aguabonita (Jordan 1892). Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Distribution: Little Kern River, California, U.S.A. [subspecies whitei]. Habitat: freshwater, brackish, marine.

willoughbii, Salmo Günther [A.] 1862:46 [10], Pl. 5 [Proceedings of the Zoological Society of London 1862 (pt 1) (art. 6) (for 11 Feb. 1862); ref. 18215] Lake Windermere, Westmorland, Scotland. Syntypes: BMNH 1862.7.26.1-2 (2). On p. 10 of separate (not verified). For spelling of specific name see Kottelat 1997:156 [ref. 22952]. Also in Günther 1863:11 [ref. 18217]. •Valid as Salvelinus willughbii (Günther 1862) -- (Frost 1966:232 [ref. 23052]). •Valid as Salvelinus willoughbii (Günther 1862) -- (Kottelat 1997:156 [ref. 22952], Kottelat & Freyhof 2007:444 [ref. 29996]). Current status: Valid as Salvelinus willoughbii (Günther 1862). Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Distribution: England. Habitat: freshwater.

zetensis, Salmothymus Hadzisce [S.] 1960:49, Fig. 3 [Izdanija, Zavod za Ribarstvo na SR Makedonija v. 3 (no. 2); ref. 13406] Zeta River near Danilovgrad, tributary to Lake Skadar, Montenegro. Syntypes: MMNHS. •Synonym of Salmothymus obtusirostris (Heckel 1851) -- (Kottelat 1997:144 [ref. 22952]). •Synonym of Salmo obtusirostris (Heckel 1851) but a doubtful subspecies -- (Snoj et al. 2002:399 [ref. 26461]). •Synonym of Salmo obtusirostris (Heckel 1851) but a valid subspecies -- (Schöffmann 2005:20 [ref. 33986]). •Valid as Salmo zetensis (Hadzisce 1960). Current status: Valid as Salmo zetensis (Hadzisce 1960). Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Distribution: Zeta River, Montenegro Habitat: freshwater.

zrmanjaensis, Salmo farioides Karaman [S.] 1938:138 [Glasnik Skopskog Nauchnog Drustva [Glasnik -- Bulletin de la Société Scientifique de Skopje]. v. 18; ref. 17197] Zrmanja River near Obrovac and Zegar, former Jugoslavian Republic of Macedonia. Syntypes: whereabouts unknown. •Synonym of Salmo trutta Linnaeus 1758, but a valid subspecies zrmanjaensis Karaman 1938 -- (Mrakovcic et al. 1995:183 [ref. 23079], Ćaleta et al. 2015:85 [ref. 34877]). •Questionably valid as Salmo zrmanjaensis Karaman 1938 -- (Kottelat 1997:143 [ref. 22952]). •Synonym of Salmo farioides Karaman 1938 -- (Bianco 2013:4 [ref. 32897]). Current status: Synonym of Salmo farioides Karaman 1938. Salmonidae: Salmoninae. Habitat: freshwater.
